Designing a complete system for handling and managing API calls can be quite complex, especially when it comes to dealing with various aspects such as IP rate limiting (identifying clients), NIP/NIPS retry strategies etc., which could cause unnecessary load on the server or data inconsistency. Therefore I'll provide you an overview of how one might tackle this task and a pseudocode for managing these requirements using Spring Boot, Java 8 streams API & RabbitMQ as queuing mechanism:

**Design Overview (Pseudocode) ** :
```pseudo-code
@RestController
public class RateLimiter {    
    private final Map<String, Sink> consumers = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();  // Consumer to sink mapping     
  	private int requestRateLimit = 10;            
      	        		         	// IP/NIP rate limit for each client.       			          	 	   	       	     				    					    public List<ConsumerRecord>  requestsList=new ArrayList() ;                    private final Sink retrySink = Sinks.retry(5)  // Retry sink with backoff strategy (exponential delay before retrying, max attempts set to avoid infinite retries).
          	   	             		      					   .add(() -> System.out.println("Retrying..."));     private final Limiter limiter;   							        				        protected RateLimiter(int requestRateLimit) {this.limiter = new ReetableRateLimiter() withInitialRefreshPeriodInMilliseconds((10/requestRateLimit))  // Set initial refresh period and maximum refill rate as per the limit
```     	     private final Function<Integer, CompletableFuture> makeRequest;          							   public RateLimiter(int requestRateLimit) { this.limiter = new ReetableRateLimiter() withInitialRefreshPeriodInMilliseconds((10 /requestRateLimit))  // Set initial refresh period and maximum refill rate as per the limit
```                                                                                                                                .add(() -> System.out.println("Retrying..."));           this.makeRequest = requestId->  {      try{          return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(doRequest());     }catch (Exception e){    throw new NonRetryableException("Failed to make a Request",e);  }}
```                                                                                                                                .add(() -> System RabbitMQTemplate rabbit =new SimpleRabbitTemplate((String)null,false,(Message message)-> 	rabbit.convertAndSend(exchangeName ,routingKey + "",message));      requestsList= new ArrayList<>(); this.makeRequest =  requestId-> {     try{       return CompletableFuture .completedFuture (doRequest()); }catch 
```                                                                                                                                Exception e){   throw    NewRetryableException("Failed to make a Request",e);}};            }}public void onCloudEvent(RateLimiterOutageEvent event) {} // This method will be called in case of retry attempts. this should handle the exception and take necessary actions

```                                                                                                                                .add(() -> System out!println("Retrying..."));  final var requestId =  UUID.randomUUID().toString(); RabbitTemplate rabbit=  new SimplestRabbitTemplatemq,String exchangeName ="rate-limit_exchange"; String routingKey

```                                                                                                                                .add(() -> System out!println("Retrying..."));  final var requestId =  requestsList.remove(0);   Future future  = makeRequest application/json}// this method will process the next message from queue       }}; public static void main (String[] args) {RateLimiter rateLimit = new Ratelimter(); // Initialize and start server, call API's to handle requests here}}
